S.C. Locke HTML Symbol Test Page

How to contact me.


I started this file simply because I wanted to have a place where I could look up any symbol that is available in html. It might be that some of the symbols are not yet standardized enough, so you might want to make sure that if you use one, that it renders properly on a few different platforms. Of course, many of the symbols would have alphabetic codes, but knowing the numeric code might even help find these alphabetic codes. (Or you could try a site such as http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/sgml/entities.html.)

The tables at the bottom were created by writing a simple excel file, with one entry to update for each ten centuries. (Not that exciting a program, but sufficient for my purposes.)
